<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">PROXY STATEMENT</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">General Information</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Use of Proxies</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This Proxy Statement is furnished in connection with the solicitation by Baldwin &amp; Lyons, Inc. (the &#8220;Corporation&#8221;) of proxies to be voted at the Annual Meeting of Shareholders to be held on Tuesday, May 10, 2011, in accordance with the foregoing notice.&#160;&#160;The Proxy Statement and accompanying proxy card were mailed to shareholders on or about April 4, 2011.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The mailing address of the Corporation&#8217;s principal office is 1099 North Meridian Street, Indianapolis, Indiana 46204.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Any proxy may be revoked by the person giving it at any time before it is voted by delivering to the Secretary of the Corporation a written notice of revocation or a duly executed proxy bearing a later date.&#160;&#160;Shares represented by a proxy, properly executed and returned to the Corporation, and not revoked, will be voted at the Annual Meeting.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Shares will be voted according to the directions of the shareholder as specified on the proxy.&#160;&#160;If no directions are given, the proxy will be voted <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">FOR</font> the election of the thirteen directors named as nominees in this Proxy Statement, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">FOR</font> the ratification of the appointment of Ernst &amp; Young LLP as independent auditors for the Corporation, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">FOR</font> approval of <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">executive officer compensation and </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">FOR</font> establishing <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">the frequency of shareholder votes to approve executive compensation as annual.</font>&#160;&#160;Any other matters that may properly come before the meeting will be acted upon by the persons named in the accompanying proxy in accordance with their discretion.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Record Date and Voting Securities</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The close of business on March 22, 2011, has been fixed as the record date for the determination of shareholders entitled to notice of and to vote at the Annual Meeting and any adjournment thereof.&#160;&#160;As of March 22, 2011, the Corporation had 2,623,109 shares of Class A Common Stock outstanding and entitled to vote.&#160;&#160;Each share of Class A Common Stock is entitled to one vote.&#160;&#160;The vote can be exercised in person or by proxy.&#160;&#160;There are no other outstanding securities of the Corporation entitled to vote.&#160;&#160;There will be no cumulative voting for the election of directors.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Shares of Class B Common Stock are not entitled to vote and proxies are not being solicited in regard to the Class B shares.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><br>
&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Expenses of Solicitation</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All expenses of the solicitation of proxies will be paid by the Corporation.&#160;&#160;Officers, directors and other employees of the Corporation may solicit proxies by telephone or by special calls.&#160;&#160;The Corporation will also reimburse brokers and other persons holding stock in their names or in the names of their nominees for their expenses in forwarding proxies and proxy material to the beneficial owners of the Corporation&#8217;s stock.</font></div>

<div><br>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In December 2002 an action initiated by the Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;Commission&#8221;) against Mr. Weil was settled simultaneously with its filing pursuant to a consent agreement entered into by Mr. Weil.&#160;&#160;The Commission alleged violations of the anti-fraud provisions of the federal securities laws arising in connection with transactions in the securities of Kaye Group, Inc. (&#8220;Kaye Group&#8221;) involving</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">material non-public information.&#160;&#160;Mr. Weil was not an officer or director of Kaye Group.&#160;&#160;The transaction cited by the Commission in its complaint involved less than one percent of the securities of Kaye Group beneficially owned by Mr. Weil and less than one-tenth of one percent of the Kaye Group&#8217;s outstanding shares.&#160;&#160;Mr. Weil consented to the entry of a final judgment of permanent injunction and other relief, including disgorgement of alleged profits in the amount of $47,000 and civil penalties of a like amount, but did not admit to nor deny any of the allegations in the Commission&#8217;s complaint.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Audit Committee</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The composition and duties of the Audit Committee are described in the Audit Committee Report found on page 23 of this Proxy Statement.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Compensation and Employee Benefits Committee</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All members of the Compensation and Employee Benefits Committee are independent as defined in both the NASDAQ listing standards and the Securities and Exchange Commission standards applicable to compensation committee members.&#160;&#160;No interlocking relationship exists between any member of the Corporation&#8217;s Compensation and Employee Benefits Committee and any member of the compensation committee of any other company, nor has any such interlocking relationship existed in the past.</font></div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>

<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">5</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The executive compensation program is administered by the Compensation and Employee Benefit Committee of the Board of Directors.&#160;&#160;This Committee oversees the administration of the Corporation&#8217;s employee benefits plans and establishes policies relating to compensation of employees.&#160;&#160;The Committee reviews all aspects of executive compensation and evaluates performance of the Corporation&#8217;s executive officers, including the Named Executive Officers of the Corporation.&#160;&#160;In addition, the Committee reviews, manages, and administers all of the stock-based compensation plans of the Corporation and, in the case of the Employee Plan, designates officers and key employees to receive options or restricted stock, and the number and terms of the options or restricted stock.&#160;&#160;All decisions by the Committee relating to the compensation of the Corporation&#8217;s executive officers are reviewed and approved by the full Board.&#160;&#160;The Corporation&#8217;s Executive Compensation Discussion and Analysis is presented beginning on page 11 of this Proxy Statement.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Investment Committee</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Investment Committee sets policy regarding composition, quality, risk and duration of the Corporation&#8217;s investment portfolios and the positioning of such portfolios in the context of the Corporation&#8217;s enterprise risk management program.&#160;&#160;The Investment Committee also approves hiring of all portfolio investment managers and evaluates the performance of each investment manager.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Strategic Planning Committee</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Strategic Planning Committee is responsible for working closely with management to identify new opportunities available to the Corporation as well as strategies for profitably expanding existing businesses and the impact of both on the Corporation&#8217;s enterprise risk management program.&#160;&#160;The Strategic Planning Committee also has oversight of the Corporation&#8217;s adherence to its budgeting, risk management and succession planning processes.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Nominating Committee</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Nominating Committee is responsible for selecting nominees for election as directors and reviewing with the Board of Directors, on an annual basis, the requisite skills and characteristics of members of the Board of Directors.&#160;&#160;An additional discussion of the responsibilities of the Nominating Committee is contained on page 25 of this Proxy Statement.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Board of Directors and Risk Management</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As a part of its oversight function, the Board monitors how management operates the Corporation, in part via its committee structure.&#160;&#160;The board evaluates strategies, reviews management reports and considers the risks involved in all of the Corporation&#8217;s insurance and investment activities.&#160;&#160;The Corporation has no single risk management committee but, rather, each committee considers risk issues associated with its specific role as discussed in this document.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Chairman and Lead Director</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Between 1997 and December, 2010, Gary W. Miller served as the Corporation&#8217;s CEO as well as its Chairman.&#160;&#160;Effective December, 2010, Mr. Miller became the Executive Chairman of the Board of Directors.&#160;&#160;In determining that Mr. Miller was the appropriate person to serve in the role of Executive Chairman, the Board relied on several important measures.&#160;&#160;Mr. Miller&#8217;s leadership, integrity and vision have been instrumental in the successful growth of the Corporation for over 40 years.&#160;&#160;He has served an active role in the Corporation&#8217;s continued strong performance, despite challenging economic and market conditions.&#160;&#160;Mr. Miller has the confidence of the Board and the Board believes that Mr. Miller, working closely with the CEO, Joseph J. DeVito, has the ability to assist Mr. DeVito and his management team in</font></div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>

<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">6</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">managing both the short and long-term strategies necessary in the challenging marketplace in which the Corporation competes.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">With the roles of Chairman and CEO separated, the Board believes that the office of Executive Chairman of the Board of Directors can function in an appropriate manner with the understanding that mechanisms are in place to ensure that the Corporation maintains the highest standards of corporate governance which insures the continued accountability of the CEO to the Board.&#160;&#160;These mechanisms include:</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The majority of directors are independent.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">

<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The election by the Board of Steven A. Shapiro to be the non-employee Lead Director.&#160;&#160;Mr. Shapiro has been a member of the Corporation&#8217;s Board since 2007, is co-chairman of the Strategic Planning Committee and a member of the Investment Committee.&#160;&#160;He has been a strong and influential member of the Board and plays an integral role in promoting confidence in the Board&#8217;s execution of its responsibilities.&#160;&#160;&#160;As detailed below in how the roles will interact, Mr. Shapiro&#8217;s responsibilities as Lead Director and his advisory role to Mr. Miller and Mr. DeVito will complement Mr. Miller&#8217;s role as Executive Chairman of the Board while providing the necessary checks and balances to hold both the Board and the Executive Chairman accountable in their respective roles.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Audit, Compensation, and Nominating Committees are comprised of and chaired by non-employee directors who meet the independence requirements under the NASDAQ listing standards and other governing laws and regulations.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

</td>

<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Review and determination of Mr. Miller&#8217;s compensation and performance will remain within the purview of the Compensation and Employee Benefits Committee.</font></div>

<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The non-employee directors will meet in regular executive sessions, without management present, to discuss the effectiveness of the Corporation&#8217;s management, the quality of the Board meetings and any other issues and concerns.</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

</td>

</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Board does not have a policy as to whether the role of the CEO and the Chairman should be separate, or whether the Chairman should be a management or non-management director.&#160;&#160;Thus, while the Board has determined that Mr. Miller will serve in the role of Executive Chairman of the Board, the Board has the right to determine, in the future,<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160;</font>if the roles will be combined or remain separate, as well as to determine whether or not a management or non-management chairman would be in the best interest of the Corporation and its stockholders.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Section&#160;16(a)&#160;Beneficial Ownership Reporting Compliance</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Section&#160;16(a)&#160;of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 requires certain executive officers, directors and ten percent (10.0%) beneficial owners to file initial reports of ownership and reports of changes in ownership of the Corporation&#8217;s securities with the Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160;&#160;Copies of those reports must be furnished to the Corporation.&#160;&#160;Based solely on a review of the Section&#160;16(a)&#160;reports furnished to the Corporation with respect to 2010 and written representations from the affected executive officers and directors, we believe that all Section&#160;16(a)&#160;filing requirements applicable to the Corporation&#8217;s executive officers and directors during 2010 were satisfied.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps">Executive Compensation Discussion And Analysis</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Introduction</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The following discussion provides an overview of the philosophy, objectives, administrative and material elements of and decisions relating to the Corporation&#8217;s Executive Compensation Program for 2010 as well as changes for 2011.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Executive Compensation Philosophy, Strategy &amp; Objectives</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Corporation&#8217;s compensation philosophy and objectives are directly related to its business strategy and objectives.&#160;&#160;The Compensation and Employee Benefit Committee of the Board (the &#8220;Committee&#8221;) believes that, in order to maximize stakeholder value, executive compensation should be aligned with business strategy in addition to financial goals.&#160;&#160;The Committee, on behalf of the full Board of Directors, believes that the Corporation&#8217;s compensation programs should:</font><br>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Create compensation which is targeted at a level that will allow the Corporation to attract, retain, and motivate top executive talent.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Ensure that an appropriate relationship exists between compensation and the creation of shareholder value.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Recognize the unique, cyclical nature of the markets in which the Corporation operates and the external factors to which the Corporation is subjected.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Recognize the significant industry experience, averaging over 30 years, of the Corporation&#8217;s Named Executive Officers.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Support long-term decision-making and, accordingly, long-term financial growth.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Include benefits and perquisites to the extent there is valid business rationale for doing so.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee believes that the compensation program in place for 2010 supported these objectives.&#160;&#160;The program for 2011 will be substantially unchanged from the 2010 program.</font></div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>

<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">11</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Executive Compensation Administration</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Role of the Compensation and Employee Benefits Committee</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee is responsible for approving all components of the compensation of the Executive Chairman, the Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;), as well as each executive reporting directly to the CEO, a group inclusive of all Named Executive Officers.&#160;&#160;The Committee administers all executive officer compensation plans, programs, and guidelines and has the final decision-making role in compensation paid to the Corporation&#8217;s executive officers.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Role of Executive Officers</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The CEO and COO, Joseph J. DeVito, sets goals and evaluates each executive officer&#8217;s performance.&#160;&#160;He makes recommendations regarding compensation to the Executive Chairman of the Board and the Committee.&#160;&#160;Neither the Executive Chairman of the Board nor the CEO has decision authority regarding his own level of compensation, nor that of any of the other executive officers.&#160;&#160;However, the CEO does participate in Committee meetings, at the Committee&#8217;s request, to provide:</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Background information regarding the Corporation&#8217;s operating results and financial objectives;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The CEO&#8217;s evaluation of the performance of the executive officers, including all of the other Named Executive Officers; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Recommendations for completed year compensation awards and future opportunities for executive officers, including all Named Executive Officers.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Role of the Committee&#8217;s Advisor</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee has the authority to engage an executive compensation consultant or other advisor as necessary to fulfill its duties to the Corporation&#8217;s shareholders.&#160;&#160;In 2008, the Corporation engaged an independent executive compensation consulting firm, to conduct an executive compensation review and provide feedback related to the Corporation&#8217;s executive compensation programs in general.&#160;&#160;Changes to executive compensation plans during 2008 and 2009 resulting from this review have been discussed in the Corporation&#8217;s Proxy Statements for the Annual Meeting of Shareholders for the meetings held May 5, 2009 and May 4, 2010, which may be obtained on the Corporation&#8217;s website at www.baldwinandlyons.com or from the SEC&#8217;s Edgar website (www.sec.gov/edgar).&#160;&#160;The Committee determined that an additional review was not necessary during 2010 as basic components of the Plan had not changed.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Corporation and Committee have developed a pay strategy that supports the Corporation&#8217;s compensation philosophy, as enumerated above, and supports execution of the Corporation&#8217;s business strategy.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">These guiding principles have been executed through the pay strategy for 2010 and are further explained below:</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Base salaries are, for the most part, above the market 75th percentile of the peer group in recognition of significant tenure and experience, and to ensure continued attraction and retention of executive talent<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">;</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Annual incentive opportunities are below the market 25th percentile of the peer group so as not to encourage engaging in short-term profit opportunities at the expense of long-term decision-making and increases in long-term shareholder value<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">;</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A percentage of annual incentive bonus for executive officers is paid in the form of the Corporation&#8217;s Class B common stock which vests over a number of years.&#160;&#160;This form of compensation not only aligns the executive&#8217;s interests with shareholders but provides retention benefits to the Corporation;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div id="HDR">

</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">

<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Long-term incentives have traditionally been delivered in the form of book value appreciation rights (&#8220;BVARs&#8221;) which focus on financial returns strongly correlated to shareholder value (BVARs are described further below); and,</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Limited perquisites are offered, primarily consisting of vehicles provided at the Corporation&#8217;s expense.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Defining the Competitive Market</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Because of the unique nature of the combination of markets in which the Corporation operates, the Committee does not believe that there are individual companies to which it can reliably compare the performance of the Corporation over a limited period of time.&#160;&#160;While the Committee has, in the past, as part of previous independent executive compensation reviews, identified companies which the Committee believed were suitable for consideration as peer companies, no such benchmarking was done in 2010.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Compensation and Risk Taking Considerations</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">One of the responsibilities of the Committee is to consult with members of the Strategic Planning and Audit Committees to consider the relationship of compensation programs to the Corporation&#8217;s financial and strategic goals.&#160;&#160;The committee reviews the balance achieved in the compensation programs related to the fact that management&#8217;s personal financial situation could be significantly impacted by the Corporation&#8217;s financial performance.&#160;&#160;Based on such inter-committee communications, the Committee believes that the executive compensation arrangements do not encourage executives to take unnecessary or excessive risks that could threaten the value of the Corporation.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The bonus hurdles selected by the Committee are based solely on operating income, rather than sales or revenue targets which could encourage the production of unprofitable business.&#160;&#160;Operating income hurdles are selected in conjunction with the full Board&#8217;s review and approval of the operating budget for the year as developed by management.&#160;&#160;Careful consideration is given to current and anticipated market conditions, including current competitive pressures and those related to the development of new products, which are expected to be encountered in the Corporation&#8217;s business operations.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee believes that the present proportion of performance-based and non-performance based compensation is balanced in such a way as to motivate the executives to fulfill the corporate mission and vision, including specific and focused performance objectives, but does not encourage unnecessary or excessive risk taking.&#160;&#160;In addition, a significant portion of executives&#8217; performance-based compensation is in the form of long-term equity incentives which do not encourage unnecessary or excessive risk because they generally vest over a three year period of time thereby focusing the executives on the Corporation&#8217;s long-term interests.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Components of Executive Compensation for 2010</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The principal components of the Corporation&#8217;s 2010 executive compensation program for executive officers, including the Named Executive Officers, were:</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Base salary;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Annual incentives;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Long-term incentives; and,</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Employee benefits and perquisites</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Each of these elements is discussed more fully below.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">13</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">

</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Base Salary</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee annually reviews and, if appropriate, adjusts each executive officer&#8217;s base salary.&#160;&#160;The Committee considers several factors when determining if a base salary adjustment is warranted and how much of an adjustment is appropriate.&#160;&#160;These factors include:</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Corporation performance against business objectives;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Changes in levels of responsibility;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Individual performance for the previous year;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Industry and general economic conditions</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">While the Committee considers these factors to guide its decisions, it does not rely on them exclusively.&#160;&#160;The Committee typically exercises significant business judgment based on an assessment of compensation levels and alignment with the Corporation&#8217;s compensation philosophy and pay strategy.&#160;&#160;The annual review of base salaries for 2010, as reported in the Proxy Statement for the Annual Meeting of Shareholders for the meeting held May 4, 2010, resulted in increases to base salaries for the Named Executive Officers by amounts ranging from 0% to 6.7% (averaging 4.1%).</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For 2011, following its annual review, the Committee has determined to increase base salaries for the Named Executive Officers by amounts ranging from 0% to 19.9% (averaging 8.1%), which the Committee believes is in line with changes in individual job responsibilities and performance.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Annual Incentives for 2010</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Corporation&#8217;s executive officers, including each of the Named Executive Officers, participated in the Corporation&#8217;s Executive Incentive Bonus Plan for 2010 (&#8220;the Plan&#8221;).&#160;&#160;A more detailed description of the Plan was included, starting on page 21, of the Proxy Statement for the Annual Meeting of Shareholders for the meeting held May 4, 2010, which may be obtained on the Corporation&#8217;s website at www.baldwinandlyons.com or from the SEC&#8217;s Edgar web site (www.sec.gov/edgar).</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Under the Plan, each participant, including each of the Named Executive Officers, was provided with a target annual incentive opportunity according to the pay strategy discussed above.&#160;&#160;Annual incentive bonuses for 2010 were determined using a preset formula-based bonus program consisting of two components: 50% was dependent upon pre-tax operating profit and 50% was dependent on an evaluation of each officer&#8217;s individual performance and changes in executive responsibilities.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For the operating profit component, the Compensation and Employee Benefit Committee (the &#8220;Committee&#8221;) established a &#8220;hurdle&#8221;.&#160;&#160;The hurdle was referenced to the planned pre-tax operating income for 2010, as approved by the Board of Directors.&#160;&#160;Fifty percent (50%) of the executive&#8217;s bonus was determined by comparing the actual pre-tax operating income for the year against the hurdle amount.&#160;&#160;That portion of the bonus may increase or decrease as actual pre-tax operating income is higher or lower than the hurdle.&#160;&#160;A range has been established with 75% of the hurdle, referred to as the &#8220;threshold&#8221; and 150% of the hurdle, referred to as &#8220;superior performance&#8221;.&#160;&#160;The formula multiplies 50% of the target bonus by the percentage difference within this range times two.&#160;&#160;Therefore, if operating income falls below the threshold, this portion of the bonus would be eliminated.&#160;&#160;If operating income equals or exceeds superior performance, the maximum portion of the bonus could be double the target.&#160;&#160;For 2010, actual operating profit was below the threshold and, accordingly, this portion of the target bonus was reduced to zero.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The individual performance component of the Plan is designed in recognition of the fact that significant contributions by certain executives to the long-term success of the Corporation may not be immediately reflected in operating income.&#160;&#160;The CEO develops performance goals for the executives in conjunction with the creation of the corporate strategic plan and, while individual performance goals vary among the executives depending on their specific responsibilities, many of these goals are inter-dependent with the</font></div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>

<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">14</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">focus of positioning the Corporation to achieve its long-term objectives.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The most significant common objective goals for 2010 included numerous activities designed to meet the goals set forth in the Corporation&#8217;s three year strategic plan, the enhancement and evolution of comprehensive performance-based management criteria for each department, formal quarterly evaluation of improvements in staff productivity and adherence to budgets.&#160;&#160;In addition, Mr. Corydon was responsible for the successful renewal of major reinsurance treaties, oversight for all &#8220;non-wheels&#8221; products, maintenance of enterprise risk management programs, financial evaluation of new business opportunities and implementation of accounting systems for all new products; Mr. Bonini was responsible for the achievement of customer relations goals for all &#8220;wheels&#8221; product lines in a difficult and highly competitive environment, including the successful renewal of all major clients, expansion of the Corporation&#8217;s brokerage business and the development of value added partnerships in the area of safety and risk selection; and Mr. Morfas was responsible for continued reduction in claim handling costs, the establishment of systematic, repeatable training programs for all claims operations, the selection and design of new comprehensive claims systems and continued improvement of in-house legal capabilities.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">In addition to overall responsibility for all of the individual goals mentioned for the executives above, Mr. DeVito&#8217;s specific goals included successful implementation of the three year strategic plan, the principal responsibility for evaluation of new business opportunities and continuance and expansion of favorable relationships with major customers and business partners.&#160;&#160;In recognition of Mr. DeVito&#8217;s success in these areas during the period 2007 through 2010, he was named Chief Executive Officer, in addition to his roles as President and Chief Operating Officer, in December, 2010.&#160;&#160;Mr. Miller, CEO until December, 2010 and now Executive Chairman of the Board of Directors, was evaluated on the successful completion of all executive officer goals as well as the effective and timely communication between management and the Board of Directors.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Determination of satisfactory achievement of individual goals is reviewed on a frequent basis through both group and individual evaluations conducted between the executives and the CEO.&#160;&#160;Achievement of all significant individual performance goals is considered when determining the discretionary component of the bonus.&#160;&#160;This component can be decreased or eliminated based on the CEO&#8217;s determination of an executive&#8217;s performance related to his or her individual goals.&#160;&#160;There is no specific percentage that each individual goal contributes to the total but, rather, it is the substantial achievement of all of the significant goals which is evaluated for each executive.&#160;&#160;For 2010, the Committee determined that the CEO substantially achieved all of his discretionary goals and, accordingly, his target bonus was awarded at 100%.&#160;&#160;The Committee also determined that the Executive Chairman largely met his goals and 77% of this target bonus was awarded.&#160;&#160;The Committee agreed with the CEO&#8217;s determination that the other Named Executive Officers, to varying degrees, achieved their significant individual goals and, accordingly, target awards for this component were awarded in the range of 69% to 100%.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All bonuses granted under the Plan were paid to executives, including the Named Executive Officers, two-thirds in cash and one-third in the form of restricted Class B common shares, in accordance with the Plan.&#160;&#160;Amounts presented in the Summary Compensation Table reflect this distribution with cash portions shown in the Bonus column and the equity component shown in the Stock Awards column.&#160;&#160;Class B common shares paid as part of the 2010 bonuses are subject to risk of forfeiture upon termination of employment for any reason other than death, disability or retirement prior to vesting.&#160;&#160;Vesting occurs ratably on the first, second and third anniversaries of the grant.&#160;&#160;Additional information regarding these restrictions is presented in the equity award tables elsewhere in this document.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Long-term Incentives for 2010</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Corporation has, in the past, granted stock options to certain executive officers and other employees of the Corporation.&#160;&#160;However, since 1997, the Committee has limited the use of the Corporation&#8217;s common stock to compensate executive officers and other employees of the Corporation, to the payment</font></div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div>
<div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>

<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">15</font></div>

<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">of a portion of annual incentive bonuses in the form of restricted Class B shares, as described elsewhere in the document.&#160;&#160;Instead, for several years the Corporation has utilized &#8220;book value appreciation rights&#8221; (BVARs) as the sole form of long-term incentives for executive officers and other management personnel.&#160;&#160;BVARs do not have any association with the market value of the Corporation&#8217;s common stock and are settled solely in cash.&#160;&#160;No equity securities are issued in connection with this form of compensation.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">BVARs provide deferred compensation to employees, including the Named Executive Officers, formulaically based on the increase in the Corporation&#8217;s book value, with certain adjustments for extra dividends paid to shareholders, over a five-year period.&#160;&#160;This program results in compensation which is directly linked to the Corporation&#8217;s performance and increases in the book value of the Corporation, closely aligning value realized from BVARs with shareholder value creation.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Increases and decreases in the value of BVARs for the Named Executives for the three year period ending December 31, 2010, resulting from changes in the Corporation&#8217;s book value, are shown in the Non-Equity Incentive Compensation column of the Summary Compensation Table.&#160;&#160;Management believes this </font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">presentation is appropriate since the BVARs are not based upon changes in the market value of equity securities and are not settled in any form of equity security.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Currently outstanding BVARs vest ratably over a three-year period, cannot be exercised prior to January 1 of the calendar year in which they expire (five years from grant), except in the case of death, disability or normal retirement.&#160;&#160;In addition, termination of employment for reasons other than death, disability or retirement results in forfeit of all vested and unvested BVARs.&#160;&#160;These plan provisions provide employee retention benefits to the Corporation.&#160;&#160;BVARs, when granted, have historically been widely distributed to virtually all salaried employees in amounts proportional to their job responsibilities and annual salary bases.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee has periodically granted BVARs but does not follow a set schedule of grants.&#160;&#160;BVARs were last awarded in 2007.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Employee Benefits and Perquisites</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Corporation offers its executive officers standard employee benefits, including the ability to participate in the group life, health, dental and disability insurance as well as the Corporation&#8217;s 401(k) Plan, to the same extent offered to all employees of the Corporation.&#160;&#160;The Corporation matches contributions made by the executive officers to the 401(k) Plan consistent with the matching contribution for all participants of the Plan.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Committee has also approved arrangements providing executive officers with the use of a Corporation-owned automobile, including maintenance costs, insurance coverage and a partial fuel allowance.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Components for 2011</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Annual Incentives for 2011</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">For 2011, the Committee has determined to maintain the structure of the annual incentive plan utilized in 2010, without modification.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Any incentives earned as a result of the 2011 annual incentive plan will be distributed early in 2012 with two-thirds paid in cash and one-third in the form of restricted stock.&#160;&#160;The total incentive earned will be determined 50% based on operating profits and 50% based on individual goals although the provisions of the Plan could result in either component being more or less than 50% of the final award.&#160;&#160;This is identical to the pro-ration used in 2010.&#160;&#160;The restricted stock portion of the bonus will be granted to each</font></div>

</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">senior executive, including the Named Executive Officers, based on the closing price of the stock on the day the award is determined.&#160;&#160;Shares will vest one-third per year over a three year period.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">A more detailed description of the Executive Bonus Plan, which was effective beginning in 2010, was included starting on page 21 of the Proxy Statement for the Annual Meeting of Shareholders for the meeting held May 4, 2010, which may be obtained on the Corporation&#8217;s website at www.baldwinandlyons.com or from the SEC Edgar website (www.sec.gov/edgar).</font></div>
